<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Item 2.02&nbsp;Results of Operations and
Financial Condition.</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On September
27, 2007, the Registrant issued a press release and held a conference call with
analysts to report on the results of operations for the third quarter of fiscal
year 2007, which ended on August 31, 2007.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Furnished with
this Form&nbsp;8-K as Exhibit&nbsp;99.1 is a copy of the press release labeled &#147;McCormick
Reports Record Third Quarter Sales and Profits,&#148; which includes an unaudited
Consolidated Income Statement for the three months ended August 31, 2007, an
unaudited Consolidated Balance Sheet of the Registrant as of August 31, 2007,
and an unaudited Consolidated Cash Flow Statement for the three months ended
August 31, 2007.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Item 9.01 Financial
Statements and Exhibits.</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)&#160; Exhibits.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The exhibit to
this report is listed in Item 2.02 above and in the Exhibit Index that follows
the signature line.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">SIGNATURES</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pursuant to the requirements of the Securities
Exchange Act of 1934, the Registrant has duly caused this report to be signed
on its behalf by the undersigned hereunto duly authorized.</font></p>

<body lang="EN-US">

<div>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit
99.1</font></b></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><img width="604" height="93" src="g247251khi001.jpg"></font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">FOR IMMEDIATE
RELEASE</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt 3.5pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">McCORMICK REPORTS RECORD THIRD
QUARTER SALES AND PROFIT</font></u></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b>Increased sales 8%.&#160; Consumer
business sales rose 9% and industrial business sales rose 7%.</b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b>Reported earnings per share of $0.43.&#160;
On a comparable basis, excluding restructuring charges, earnings per
share increased 7% to $0.45.</b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b>Reaffirmed expectation to increase earnings per share 9-11% for fiscal
year 2007 on a comparable basis.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">SPARKS,
MD, SEPTEMBER 27&#151;McCormick &amp; Company, Incorporated (NYSE:MKC), today reported
record results for the third quarter ended August 31, 2007 and reaffirmed
guidance for the fiscal year.&#160; For the
third quarter, earnings per share were $0.43 compared to $0.32 in the prior
year.&#160; On a comparable basis, excluding
restructuring charges, the Company increased earnings per share 7% to $0.45 in
the third quarter of 2007, compared to earnings per share of $0.42 a year ago.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Robert
J. Lawless, Chairman and CEO, commented, &#147;We were pleased to achieve strong
sales increases in both domestic and international markets.&#160; Despite higher material costs, our net income
and earnings per share were on target.&#160;
For the 2007 fiscal year we reaffirm our expectations to grow sales 5-7%
and increase earnings per share 9-11% on a comparable basis.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Sales
in the third quarter rose 8%, which was an increase of 6% in local
currency.&#160; The Company increased sales
significantly in international markets with a 12% increase in Europe and a 21%
increase in the Asia/Pacific region.&#160; The
increases were primarily from favorable foreign exchange rates as well as
higher volume.&#160; Sales in North America
rose 6% due to favorable price and product mix as well as higher volume.&#160; In the U.S. consumer business, a portion of
the third quarter volume increase related to an estimated $9-11 million of
earlier shipments for the fall season.&#160;
The elimination of lower margin business reduced sales 1% during the
third quarter of 2007.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A
decrease of 0.9 percentage points in gross profit margin was primarily due to
the impact of higher material costs on the industrial business.&#160; The impact of these higher costs on margin
more than offset the benefit of savings from the Company&#146;s restructuring
program that are being realized in 2007.&#160;
While the Company continues to take pricing actions to offset increased
material costs, gross profit margin will continue to be under pressure through
the remainder of fiscal year 2007. Selling, general and administrative expense
was favorably impacted by cost savings as well as lower incentive compensation
expense in the third quarter of 2007.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Earnings
per share were $0.43 compared to $0.32 in the third quarter of 2006.&#160; Charges related to the Company&#146;s
restructuring program decreased earnings per share $0.02 in the third </font></p>

<br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\fc\26914272175_D11624_2429594\24725-1-kh.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Sep 26 14:27 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">quarter of 2007
compared to $0.10 in the third quarter of 2006.&#160;
Excluding these impacts in both periods, earnings per share rose $0.03
driven by sales growth and higher operating income margin.&#160; The unfavorable impacts of a higher tax rate
and increased interest expense were offset in part by lower average shares
outstanding.&#160; The Company increased its
pace of share buyback activity during the third quarter with repurchases of $89
million compared to $28 million in the third quarter of 2006 bringing the year-to-date
repurchases to $147 million.&#160; It also
reaffirmed its guidance for share repurchases of up to $180 million in 2007.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
the 2007 fiscal year, on a comparable basis, which excludes the impact of
restructuring charges, the Company expects to grow earnings per share 9-11% in
2007.&#160; Including estimated restructuring
charges of $0.18, 2007 earnings per share are projected to be in the range of
$1.69-$1.73.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Mr.
Lawless further stated, &#147;We are on track for 2007 to be another record year at
McCormick.&#160; We have passed the half-way
point of our 3-year restructuring program and are realizing cost savings from
our actions to simplify our business and improve profitability.&#160; Both our consumer and industrial segments are
benefiting from this program, as well as the key growth initiatives that are
driving sales with innovative new products, revitalization of our core products
and more effective marketing.&#160; This
progress is a testament to the capabilities, energy and effort of McCormick
employees around the world.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Business
Segment Results</font></b></p>

<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="border-collapse:collapse;width:100.0%;">

  </td>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In
the third quarter, sales for McCormick&#146;s consumer business rose 9%, which was
an increase of 6% in local currency.&#160; The
increase was led by higher volume that included an estimated 2-3% benefit related
to earlier shipments for the fall season when compared to the third quarter of
2006.&#160; In addition to higher volume,
favorable price and product mix also increased sales.&#160; Consumer sales in the Americas rose 8% and 7%
in local currency.&#160; Earlier shipments for
the fall season added an estimated 4-5% to sales.&#160;&#160;&#160; The Company grew sales of Hispanic items,
seafood complements, Zatarain&#146;s brand and gourmet products in the U.S. and the
Club House brand in Canada.&#160; Consumer
sales in Europe increased 10%, which was an increase of 3% in local
currency.&#160; Increases in the U.K. and
France were achieved with marketing support behind branded products and pricing
actions.&#160; In the Asia/Pacific region,
sales rose 11%, which was an increase of 1% in local currency.&#160; Double-digit sales growth in China was
largely offset by poor sales performance in Australia.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In
the third quarter, consumer business operating income excluding restructuring
charges rose to $70.5&nbsp;million from $60.7&nbsp;million in 2006.&#160; This was an increase of 16%, driven primarily
by higher sales and lower selling, general and administrative expense.</font></p>

<br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In
the third quarter, sales for McCormick&#146;s industrial business increased 7%,
which was an increase of 5% in local currency.&#160;
The impact of the Company&#146;s actions to eliminate lower margin customers
and products reduced sales in the third quarter by 2%.&#160; The remaining increase of 7% had equal
contributions from volume and from price and product mix.&#160; Industrial sales in the Americas rose 3%,
which was an increase of 2% in local currency.&#160;
The elimination of lower margin customers and products in this part of
the industrial business reduced sales 2%.&#160;
Higher sales were driven largely by price increases related to higher
material costs.&#160; Increased volume of
snack seasonings and new products for large food manufacturers were offset by
lower demand from restaurant customers that was related to general industry
weakness.&#160; In Europe, industrial sales
rose 16%, which was an increase of 9% in local currency, with continued
strength in sales of condiments and of seasonings for snack products.&#160; In addition, sales of branded food service
products in the U.K. contributed to the increase.&#160; In this region, the elimination of lower
margin customers reduced sales 2%.&#160; Sales
in the Asia/Pacific region rose 27%, which was an increase of 19% in local
currency, with significant gains in both China and Australia.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In
the third quarter, industrial business operating income excluding restructuring
charges was $22.6 million compared to $22.7 million in 2006.&#160; The benefit of higher sales and lower
selling, general and administrative expense was offset by significant increases
in several commodities.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Non-GAAP
Financial Measures</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The pro forma information excluding restructuring
charges in this press release are not measures that are defined in generally
accepted accounting principles (&#147;GAAP&#148;).&#160;
Management believes the pro forma information is important for purposes
of comparison to prior periods and development of future projections and
earnings growth prospects.&#160; This
information is also used by management to measure the profitability of our
on-going operations.&#160; Management analyzes
the Company&#146;s business performance and trends excluding amounts related to the
restructuring.&#160; These measures provide a
more consistent view of performance than the closest GAAP equivalent for
management and investors.&#160; Management
compensates for this by using these measures in combination with the GAAP
measures.&#160; The presentation of the
non-GAAP measures in this press release are made alongside the most directly
comparable GAAP measures.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Pro
forma Information</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Company has provided below certain pro forma financial results excluding
amounts related to a restructuring program in 2007 and 2006.</font></p>

that could be materially affected by external factors such as:&#160; actions of competitors, customer
relationships, ability to realize expected cost savings and margin
improvements, market acceptance of new products, actual amount and timing of
special charge items, removal and disposal costs, final negotiations of
third-party contracts, the impact of the stock market conditions on its share
repurchase program, fluctuations in the cost and availability of supply chain
resources and global economic conditions, including interest and currency rate
fluctuations, and inflation rates.&#160;

forward-looking statements.&#160; The Company

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About
McCormick</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">McCormick
&amp; Company, Incorporated is the global leader in the manufacture, marketing
and distribution of spices, seasonings and flavors to the entire food industry&#151;to
foodservice and food manufacturers as well as to retail outlets.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">#&nbsp;&nbsp;#&nbsp;&nbsp;#</font></p>

john_mccormick@mccormick.com)<br>

(410-771-7244 or joyce_brooks@mccormick.com)<br>
